    id: string
    edition: Edition
    moment: string
    creator: Person
  }

  interface Person {
    id: string
    name: string
  }

  interface Comment {
    id: string
    creator: Person
    message: string
    moment: string
  }

  interface Request {
    id: string
    creator: Person
    moment: string
    edition: Edition
    status: 'review' | 'acepted' | 'rejected'
    type: 'create' | 'change' | 'split' | 'join'

  interface Edition {
    id: string
    content: string
    request: null | Request
    prev: null | Edition
    next: null | Edition
  }
